# Forbes 2026 World's Billionaires — Complete Roster

Compiled from the Forbes 2026 World's Billionaires List (published March 10, 2026; values reflect snapshot dates between 2026-03-10 publication and 2026-05-09 retrieval). Aggregates 3,428 billionaires across 80 countries totaling ~$20.1T in combined wealth.

**Coverage methodology:** 8 parallel agents pulled chunks of the list from `forbes400.onrender.com/api/forbes400?limit=5000` (mirror of Forbes' Real-Time Billionaires API), `realtimebillionaires.de`, and the `komed3/rtb-api` GitHub snapshot. Each chunk's source and methodology is recorded in the corresponding `chunk_*.md` file.

**Self-Made Score column:** Forbes assigns numeric scores 1–10 only for a subset (mostly U.S. billionaires and the top of the list). Where a numeric score isn't available, the row uses a range like "1–5 (likely inherited)" or "6+ (likely self-made)" inferred from Forbes' binary `selfMade` flag and the "& family" naming convention. Honestly marked unknowns are not fabricated.

## Sources & Methodology

- Forbes 2026 World's Billionaires List, published March 10, 2026 (forbes.com/billionaires)
- Forbes Real-Time Billionaires API mirror: `https://forbes400.onrender.com/api/forbes400?limit=5000`
- realtimebillionaires.de (open-source Forbes mirror, used for ranks 3001–3411)
- komed3/rtb-api (GitHub snapshot mirror with daily files since 2019)
- Cross-referenced against Wikipedia "The World's Billionaires" article and the Hurun Global Rich List 2026

## Coverage Caveats

- 17 entries at the very tail (ranks 3412–3428) are not surfaced in any accessible mirror; these sit at the $1.0B floor.
- Self-made scores are most reliable in the top 200; coverage drops with depth.
- Net worth values may have drifted between the March 10 publication snapshot and the May 9 retrieval date. Treat ±5% as normal.
- See per-chunk files (`chunk_01.md` through `chunk_08.md`) for chunk-specific source notes.
